        <h2>Storyline</h2>
        
        <div class="inline canwrap" itemprop="description">
            <p>
The evil Trade Federation, led by Nute Gunray is planning to take over the peaceful world of Naboo. Jedi Knights Qui-Gon Jinn and Obi-Wan Kenobi are sent to confront the leaders. But not everything goes to plan. The two Jedi escape, and along with their new Gungan friend, Jar Jar Binks head to Naboo to warn Queen Amidala, but droids have already started to capture Naboo and the Queen is not safe there. Eventually, they land on Tatooine, where they become friends with a young boy known as Anakin Skywalker. Qui-Gon is curious about the boy, and sees a bright future for him. The group must now find a way of getting to Coruscant and to finally solve this trade dispute, but there is someone else hiding in the shadows. Are the Sith really extinct? Is the Queen really who she says she is? And what's so special about this young boy?                <em class="nobr">Written by
<a href="/search/title?plot_author=simon&view=simple&sort=alpha&ref_=tt_stry_pl"
>simon</a></em>            </p>
        </div>

    <div id="titleDidYouKnow" class="article">
    <span class=rightcornerlink >
            <a href="/register/login?why=edit&ref_=tt_trv_trv"
rel="login">Edit</a>
    </span>
        <h2>Did You Know?</h2>
    <div id="trivia" class="txt-block">
        <h4>Trivia</h4>


In both of his identities, Darth Sidious/Palpatine makes his first appearance as a hologram. This is in keeping with the original trilogy, when his first appearance was a holographic communication with Darth Vader in <a href="/title/tt0080684?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Das Imperium schl&auml;gt zur&uuml;ck</a> (1980).        <a href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />
     <div id="goofs"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Goofs</h4>
When Anakin is being lifted up by Qui Gon Jinn after the pod race, he cheers &quot;Mum, I did it! YEAH!&quot; He says this before his mouth moves.        <a href="trivia?tab=gf&ref_=tt_trv_gf"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>   
                <hr />
    <div id="quotes" class="text-block">
        <h4>Quotes</h4>
[<span class="fine">first lines</span>]
<br /><a href="/name/nm0000553/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"
><span class="character">Qui-Gon Jinn</span></a>:
Captain.
<br /><a href="/name/nm0302345/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"
><span class="character">Radiant VII captain</span></a>:
Yes, sir?
<br /><a href="/name/nm0000553/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"
><span class="character">Qui-Gon Jinn</span></a>:
Tell them we wish to board at once.
<br /><a href="/name/nm0302345/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"
><span class="character">Radiant VII captain</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">to communication device</span>]
With all due respect, the ambassadors for the Supreme Chancellor wish to board immediately.
<br /><a href="/name/nm0141324/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"
><span class="character">Nute Gunray</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">on view screen</span>]
Yes, of course. As you know, our blockade is perfectly legal and we'd be happy to receive the ambassadors.
<br />        <a href="trivia?tab=qt&ref_=tt_trv_qu"
class="nobr" >See more</a> &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />
     <div id="crazyCredits"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Crazy Credits</h4>
<a href="/name/nm0698681?ref_=tt_trv_cc">Greg Proops</a>' and <a href="/name/nm0135750?ref_=tt_trv_cc">Scott Capurro</a>'s credits are reversed. Proops plays Beed Annodue, the red, English-speaking pod-race announcer, and Capurro plays Fode Annodue, the green, Huttese-speaking announcer.        <a href="trivia?tab=cz&ref_=tt_trv_cc"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>

    <div class="article" id="titleUserReviewsTeaser">
        <h2>User Reviews</h2>
        <div class="user-comments">
                    <div class="tinystarbar" title="7/10">
                        <div style="width: 70px;">&nbsp;</div>
                    </div>
                <span itemprop="review" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">  
                    <strong itemprop="name">Too many &quot;Yes Men&quot; around George Lucas</strong>
                    <span itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                        <meta itemprop="worstRating" content = "1" />
                        <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="7" />
                        <meta itemprop="bestRating" content="10" />
                    </span>
                    <div class="comment-meta">
                        7 October 2001 | by <a href="/user/ur1383008/?ref_=tt_urv"
><span itemprop="author">JohnIL</span></a>
                        <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2001-10-07" />
                        &ndash; <a href="/user/ur1383008/comments?ref_=tt_urv"
>See all my reviews</a>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <p itemprop="reviewBody"><br /><br />Of course this movie had a ton of hype and what movie can live up to all of that....yada yada yada. Even allowing for that, this movie is somewhat of a dissapointment. This movie proves that it wasn't just special FX that made &quot;Star Wars&quot; fun to watch. It was as if George Lucas was so thrilled with what he could do with CGI effects, he forgot what made the original trilogy so great, which is writing and characters. It's not a bad film but the problems are many.<br /><br />-Many people have forgiven this movie for being lackluster as they say &quot;It is only the first in another trilogy and it is just setting up everything to follow&quot;. WRONG WRONG WRONG, this film needed to be it's own movie first and foremost as the other three films were. It needed to have good characters and a somewhat interesting story....it didn't.<br /><br />-The conflict in this story revolves around a trade dispute and the fate of the planet Naboo. Was anybody really caring about this? The details of the dispute are somewhat vague and what is revealed doesn't real generate enough interest for us to root for a particular side. The important conflict regarding Darth Sideous and his rise is kept far far in the background. We don't even know why Darth Maul hates the Jedi's so much....he just does. Possibly Lucas wanted Darth Maul to be somewhat like Boba Fett (silent and mysterious). It worked with Boba Fett because he was only a supporting character, not a main villian. This film really has no clear villian. I wish somebody would have had the courage and just told Lucas that his basic story was lousy.<br /><br />-Nobody looks particularly happy in this film. Qui-gon is really the only character that can be related to and even he is rather distant. The queen acts like a mannequin in much of her scenes (and looks like one to). Obi-wan Kenobi wanders through the entire movie to no avail and never says anything interesting. The characters never seem to talk about anything besides the plot (unlike in the first film).  C3PO and R2-D2 were pretty pointless. The Jedi council comes across as extremely cold and buracratic. And I will never understand WHY they wrote Annakin as a grade school kid in this film. He should have been a teenager. His scenes with the queen were awkward. We're not even going to discuss Jar Jar.<br /><br />Various other things...<br /><br />-The &quot;midochlorians&quot; thing seems to have just been tacked on. The humor falls flat unless you are an extremely small child. Annakin destroys the trade ship at the end and safves everyone, basically BY MISTAKE!!! ILM and George Lucas seem to be so happy with their new CGI toys that they spent 95% of their time perfecting them. Quite frankly I thought the FX in &quot;Return of the Jedi&quot; were sharper, more dimensional and less cartoonish. Nothing all that memorable seems to happen here. This movie may never have been as good as the hype, but it could have easily been much better than this. I waited so long for this film, yet the first time I saw this movie I was actually bored in the middle of it.<br /><br />There are good moments. The pod race was fun, as was the light sabre battle at the end. There are some very nice special effects throughout.<br /><br /> Hopefully Lucas just had writers block when he wrote this one. Maybe he will remember what made the other films so good in time for &quot;Episode II&quot;. Though he seems to have botched the title of it already. </p>
                    </div>
                </span>
                <hr />
                <div class="yn" id="ynd_482050">
                    443 of 570 people found this review helpful.&nbsp;

                    <button class="btn small" value="No" name="ynb_482050_no" onclick="CS.TMD.user_review_vote(482050, 'tt0120915', 'no');" >No</button>
                </div>

    var pageLoaded = function() {
        if (window.jQuery) {
